[30;1m19 | [0m[35mtedious to achieve by writing stream filters by hand. The approach of chaining[0m
[30;1m20 | [0m[35mnode selection and transformation has been inspired by the `jQuery`_ Javascript[0m
[30;1m21 | [0m[35mlibrary.[0m
[30;1m22 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m23 | [0m[35m .. _`jQuery`: http://jquery.com/[0m
